2.1.1.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:generic-debug/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:generic-debug/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:generic-debug/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:generic-debug/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:generic-debug/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.GenericDebug.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__GenericDebug__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_GenericDebug_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.4.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:generic-warning/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:generic-warning/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:generic-warning/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:generic-warning/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:generic-warning/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.GenericWarning.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__GenericWarning__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_GenericWarning_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.7.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:download-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:download-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:download-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:download-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:download-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.DownloadError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_DownloadError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__DownloadError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_DownloadError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_DownloadError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_DownloadError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_OnboardError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.12.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-validation/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardDescriptorValidation.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardDescriptorValidation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardDescriptorValidation__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardDescriptorValidation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_OnboardDescriptorValidation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.15.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-format-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-format-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-format-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-format-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-format-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardDescriptorFormatError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardDescriptorFormatError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardDescriptorFormatError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardDescriptorFormatError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.17.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-unsupported-media-type/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardUnsupportedMediaType.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardUnsupportedMediaType_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardUnsupportedMediaType__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardUnsupportedMediaType_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardUnsupportedMediaType_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.20.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-unreadable-headers/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-unreadable-headers/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-unreadable-headers/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-unreadable-headers/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-unreadable-headers/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardUnreadableHeaders.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardUnreadableHeaders_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardUnreadableHeaders__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardUnreadableHeaders_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_OnboardUnreadableHeaders_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.22.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-extraction-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardExtractionError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardExtractionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardExtractionError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.25.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-checksum-mismatch/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-checksum-mismatch/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-checksum-mismatch/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-checksum-mismatch/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-checksum-mismatch/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardChecksumMismatch.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardChecksumMismatch_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardChecksumMismatch__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardChecksumMismatch_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_OnboardChecksumMismatch_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardChecksumMismatch_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-exists-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-exists-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-exists-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-package-exists-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-package-exists-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier

2.1.28.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves

    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use

2.1.30.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-onboard/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-onboard/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-onboard/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-onboard/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-descriptor-onboard/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardDescriptorOnboard.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardDescriptorOnboard_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardDescriptorOnboard__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardDescriptorOnboard_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.33.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-upload/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-upload/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-upload/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-package-upload/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-package-upload/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardPackageUpload.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardPackageUpload_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__OnboardPackageUpload__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_OnboardPackageUpload_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.35.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:onboard-package-validation/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-package-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:onboard-package-validation/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.OnboardPackageValidation.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_OnboardPackageValidation_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.38.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:update-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:update-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:update-unsupported-media-type/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-unsupported-media-type/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.UpdateUnsupportedMediaType.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_UpdateUnsupportedMediaType_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__UpdateUnsupportedMediaType__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_UpdateUnsupportedMediaType_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_UpdateUnsupportedMediaType_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_UpdateUnsupportedMediaType_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.41.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:update-package-not-found-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:update-package-not-found-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:update-package-not-found-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-package-not-found-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-package-not-found-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.UpdatePackageNotFoundError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_UpdatePackageNotFoundError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__UpdatePackageNotFoundError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_UpdatePackageNotFoundError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_UpdatePackageNotFoundError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_UpdatePackageNotFoundError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.43.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:update-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:update-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:update-extraction-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-extraction-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.UpdateExtractionError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_UpdateExtractionError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__UpdateExtractionError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.46.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:update-unreadable-package/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:update-unreadable-package/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:update-unreadable-package/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-unreadable-package/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-unreadable-package/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.UpdateUnreadablePackage.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_UpdateUnreadablePackage_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__UpdateUnreadablePackage__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers

2.1.49.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:update-script-upload-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:update-script-upload-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:update-script-upload-error/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-script-upload-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-script-upload-error/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.UpdateScriptUploadError.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_UpdateScriptUploadError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__UpdateScriptUploadError__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_UpdateScriptUploadError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_UpdateScriptUploadError_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier

2.1.51.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:update-success/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:update-success/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:update-success/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-success/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-success/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.UpdateSuccess.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_UpdateSuccess_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__UpdateSuccess__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier

2.1.54.1.3  container uploader-log:call-identifier
  Description
    Each call in Riftware is assigned a callid which is unique
    in the context of the entity making the assignment. The
    same call-id could be assigned by different entities - in
    which case, the group-call-id is used in conjunction with
    call id to provide uniqueness
  Leaves
    name: callid, type: UINT64, description: The callid is defined as a grouping with a leaf that represents
    the callid. This helps in RIFTWARE use a common tag for call-id
    in all further uses of this grouping.
    name: groupcallid, type: UINT64, description: The group call id is used to uniquely identify the assigner of
    a call id. Each entity generating call id within RIFTWARE uses
    group ids that are different from each other. A single entity
    could use multiple group ids - The caveat being that none of
    these group ids should be avaialble for other entities to use
  XPath Path
    /uploader-log:update-descriptor-update/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  XPath Keyed Path
    /uploader-log:update-descriptor-update/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW.REST URI Path
    /uploader-log:update-descriptor-update/template_params/call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-descriptor-update/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  RW Keyspec XPath Keyed Path
    N,/uploader-log:update-descriptor-update/uploader-log:template_params/uploader-log:call-identifier
  Protobuf Type
    .uploader_log.YangNotif.UploaderLog.UpdateDescriptorUpdate.TemplateParams.CallIdentifier
  Python Proto-GI Type
    UploaderLogYang.YangNotif_UploaderLog_UpdateDescriptorUpdate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  C Protobuf-C Struct Type
    UploaderLog__YangNotif__UploaderLog__UpdateDescriptorUpdate__TemplateParams__CallIdentifier
  C RWPB Identifiers
    UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_UpdateDescriptorUpdate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
    UploaderLog_notif_UpdateDescriptorUpdate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
  YPBC Base Identifier
    rw_ypbc_UploaderLog_UploaderLog_notif_UpdateDescriptorUpdate_TemplateParams_CallIdentifier
